 -|----/|____\|____|_________|_________|____\|____|____\_____|_______|\----|-
  |                                                                        |
  |                                                                        |
  |    you`re surprised? this huge piece of ascii is another piece of      |
  |    great puzzle. the game starts here. rules? you must to find an      |
  | special key-word (five alphanumeric signs). cut the main part of the   |
  |   collection, save it into the file as "encore.txt" and then try to    |
  |    decrunch with one of well-known packers (including various xpk      |
  |  libraries =). when you find the right cruncher then try to hack the   |
  |password. a tip? it`s five numers only, ehehe =) after decrunching you  |
  |will see my contribution to your perseverance - "encore" with it`s full |
  |flavour. now start your play and !MAINLY! have as much fun as you can.  |
  |                                                                        |
